Hello Dave.  I wanted to give you some general comments before tomorrow's m=
tg.  Please see below:


1.    Resolution and agreement - The start date will be 2018, what month is=
 unknown at this time.  Other comments are straight forward.

2.    Budget - I think the agreement will need some language for budget pur=
poses, such as: "This agreement is for the services specified in an amount =
not to exceed $.... for the year of 2018."    Also, certain officer 'other =
expenses' are not mentioned, including but not limited to:
Guns
Ammunition
Body cameras
Body armor
Uniforms
Cleaning uniforms
Recruiting costs
Physicals/psych examines
Radios and related communication equipment

        I think we will also need to more accurately quantify the additiona=
l:  payroll, Joint Insurance Fund, and other indirect costs as well as how =
we apply COLAs, etc.


3.    Township Liaison, Board Liaison, Operation Review Committee - I would=
 appreciate a better understand how you see these liaisons working and if a=
ny, relationship between them is planned.

I look forward to our discussion tomorrow.

Thanks, Anthony
